//G3SG1
"Weapon_G3SG1.Single"
{
	"channel"		"CHAN_STATIC"
	"volume"		"1.0"
	"pitch"			"PITCH_NORM"
	"soundlevel"  		"SNDLVL_93dB"
	//"wave"			")weapons/g3sg1/g3sg1-1.wav"
	
	"rndwave"
	{
		"wave"	"~)weapons/g3sg1/g3sg1_01.wav"
		"wave"	"~)weapons/g3sg1/g3sg1_02.wav"
		"wave"	"~)weapons/g3sg1/g3sg1_03.wav"
	}

	"soundentry_version" "2"
	"operator_stacks"
	{
		"start_stack"
		{
			
			"import_stack" "CS_distance_weapon_start"
			
			"play_distant_version_1"
			{
				"entry_name" "Weapon_G3SG1.SingleDistant"
			}
		}

		"update_stack"
		{
			"import_stack" "CS_update_weapon"
			"mixer"
			{
				"mixgroup" "WeaponsLoud"
			}
			"volume_distance_xfade"
			{
				"input_map_min" "0.0"
				"input_map_max" "1.0"
			}
			
			"speakers_spatialize"
			{
				// time as a percentage to start lerping toward stereo spread
				"input_time_start_stereo_spread" "0.1"
				// time as a percentage of wav length to stop lerping toward stereo spread
				"input_time_finish_stereo_spread" "0.3"
				// the degree of stereo-ness once the lerp has finished. 1 is full stereo, 0 is full mono 3d positional.
				"input_final_stereo_spread" "0.8"
			}
		}
	}
}

			"import_stack" "CS_update_weapon"
			"mixer"
			{
				"mixgroup" "WeaponsLoud"
			}
			"volume_distance_xfade"
			{
				"input_map_min" "0.0"
				"input_map_max" "1.0"
			}
			
			"speakers_spatialize"
			{
				// time as a percentage to start lerping toward stereo spread
				"input_time_start_stereo_spread" "0.1"
				// time as a percentage of wav length to stop lerping toward stereo spread
				"input_time_finish_stereo_spread" "0.3"
				// the degree of stereo-ness once the lerp has finished. 1 is full stereo, 0 is full mono 3d positional.
				"input_final_stereo_spread" "0.8"
			}
		}
	}
}

	"soundlevel"  		"SNDLVL_93dB"
	//"wave"			")weapons/scar20/scar20_01.wav"
	
	"rndwave"
	{
		"wave"		"~weapons/scar20/scar20_01.wav"
		"wave"		"~weapons/scar20/scar20_02.wav"
		"wave"		"~weapons/scar20/scar20_03.wav"
	}

	"soundentry_version" "2"
	"operator_stacks"
	{
		"start_stack"
		{
			
			"import_stack" "CS_distance_weapon_start"
			
			"play_distant_version_1"
			{
				"entry_name" "Weapon_SCAR20.SingleDistant"
			}
		}

		"update_stack"
		{
			"import_stack" "CS_update_weapon"
			"mixer"
			{
				"mixgroup" "WeaponsLoud"
			}
			"volume_distance_xfade"
			{
				"input_map_min" "0.0"
				"input_map_max" "1.0"
			}
			
			"speakers_spatialize"
			{
				// time as a percentage to start lerping toward stereo spread
				"input_time_start_stereo_spread" "0.1"
				// time as a percentage of wav length to stop lerping toward stereo spread
				"input_time_finish_stereo_spread" "0.3"
				// the degree of stereo-ness once the lerp has finished. 1 is full stereo, 0 is full mono 3d positional.
				"input_final_stereo_spread" "0.8"
			}
		}
	}
	
}

//AWP
"Weapon_AWP.Single"
{
	"channel"		"CHAN_STATIC"
	"volume"		"1.0"
	"pitch"			"PITCH_NORM"
	"soundlevel"  		"SNDLVL_93dB"
	//"wave"			")weapons/awp/awp1.wav"
	
	"rndwave"
	{
		"wave"	"~)weapons/awp/awp_01.wav"
		"wave"	"~)weapons/awp/awp_02.wav"
	}

	"soundentry_version" "2"
	"operator_stacks"
	{
		"start_stack"
		{
			
			"import_stack" "CS_distance_weapon_start"
			
			"play_distant_version_1"
			{
				"entry_name" "Weapon_AWP.SingleDistant"
			}
		}

		"update_stack"
		{
			"import_stack" "CS_update_weapon"
			"mixer"
			{
				"mixgroup" "WeaponsLoud"
			}
			"volume_distance_xfade"
			{
				"input_map_min" "0.0"
				"input_map_max" "1.0"
			}
			"speakers_spatialize"
			{
				// time as a percentage to start lerping toward stereo spread
				"input_time_start_stereo_spread" "0.3"
				// time as a percentage of wav length to stop lerping toward stereo spread
				"input_time_finish_stereo_spread" "0.4"
				// the degree of stereo-ness once the lerp has finished. 1 is full stereo, 0 is full mono 3d positional.
				"input_final_stereo_spread" "0.8"
			}

		}
	}
}

"Weapon_AWP.SingleDistant"
{
	"channel"		"CHAN_STATIC"
	"volume"		"1.0"
	"pitch"			"PITCH_NORM"
	"soundlevel"  		"SNDLVL_94dB"
	"wave"			"~weapons/awp/awp_distant.wav"

	"soundentry_version" "2"

	"operator_stacks"
	{
		"start_stack"
		{
			"import_stack" "CS_limit_start"
		}

		"update_stack"
		{
			"import_stack" "CS_update_weapon"
			"mixer"
			{
				"mixgroup" "DistWeapons"
			}
			"speakers_spatialize"
			{
				// time as a percentage to start lerping toward stereo spread
				"input_time_start_stereo_spread" "0.1"
				// time as a percentage of wav length to stop lerping toward stereo spread
				"input_time_finish_stereo_spread" "0.2"
				// the degree of stereo-ness once the lerp has finished. 1 is full stereo, 0 is full mono 3d positional.
				"input_final_stereo_spread" "1.0"
			}

		}
	}
}
